Oweruza a boma akufuna omwe akuimbidwa mlandu wochita zauchigawenga ku NYC alandile chigamulo chachilendo cha imfa
Oweruza ku New York City akufuna kuti a Sayfullo Saipov alandire chilango cha imfa, mmene akuimbidwa mlandu wochita zauchigawenga ku NYC ndikupha anthu asanu ndi atatu --chigamulo chachilendo chomwe sichinaperekedwe ndi khothi la boma kuyambira 1953.
Saipov, wazaka 30, akuti adagwiritsa ntchito galimoto yobwereka ku Home Depot kuchita zauchigawenga m’msewu wa njinga pafupi ndi msewu mkulu wa West Side Highway ku Lower Manhattan, ndikupha oyenda pansi komanso oyenda pa njinga mmsewuwo mu mwezi wa October.
Potsimikizira kuyenera kwa chilango cha imfa, oweluza milandu akuyenera kupereka umboni wa kuti Saipov "mwadala" adapha anthu asanu ndi atatuwo ndipo "mwadala" adavulaza kwambiri ena, malinga ndi lamulo lokhudza pempho la chigamulo chimenechi, lomwe lidaperekedwa ku Southern District ku New York.
Milandu yonseyi imakhala ndi chilango cha imfa, malinga ndi chikalata chakhothi.
Patatha milungu ingapo pachitika mlanduyi, bwalo lalikulu lamilandu linapeza Saipov ali ndi milandu 22 yophatikizapo milandu isanu ndi itatu yakupha pogwiritsa ntchito njira zachinyengo, zimene oweruza a bwalo lalikulu amagwiritsa ntchito pamilandu yochitidwa mwadala monga imeneyi, komanso mlandu wa chiwawa ndi mlandu wa kuwononga magalimoto.
Mlanduwo "udakonzedwa mosamala komanso kulingaliridwa bwino," oweruza adatero, pofotokoza momwe Saipov adachitiramo mlandu "yowopsa, yankhanza komanso yoyipa kwambiri."
"Sayfullo Habibullaevic Saipov adavulaza ena, komanso kupangitsa chisoni kwa abale ndi abwenzi a Diego Enrique Angelini, Nicholas Cleves, Ann-Laure Decadt, Darren Drake, Ariel Erlij, Hernan Ferruchi, Hernan Diego Mendoza, ndi Alejandro Damian Pagnucco," pempho lokhudza chigamulocho latero.
Anthu asanu mwa omwe anakhudzidwawo anali alendo ochokera ku Argentina.
Patha zaka 10 kuchokera pomwe khothi la ku Southern District of New York lidapereka chigamulo cha kuphedwa.
Woweruzidwayo, Khalid Barnes, adapezeka ali ndi mlandu wakupha anthu awiri ogulitsa mankhwala osokoneza bongo koma pomalizira pake adaweruzidwa kuti akhale m'ndende kwa moyo wake wonse mu September 2009.
Nthawi yomalizira kuperekedwa kwa chigamulo cha imfa mu m’mzinda wa New York inali chaka cha 1953 kwa a Julius ndi Ethel Rosenberg, okwatirana omwe adaphedwa ataweruzidwa kuti apanga ukazitape ku boma la Soviet Union pa nthawi ya Nkhondo yo Kopa kapena Cold War zaka ziwiri zapitazo.
Awiriwa okwatirana a m’banja la Rosenberg adaphedwa ndi mpando wamagetsi pa June 19, 1953.
Saipov, mbadwa ya Uzbekistan, adawonetsa kusakhudzidwa ndi zomwe adachita m'masiku ndi miyezi yotsatirayi, malinga ndi zikalata zaku khothi.
Adauza ofufuza kuti akumva bwino ndi zomwe adachitazo, apolisi atero.
Saipov adauza akuluakulu aboma kuti adalimbikitsidwa kuti achite izi atawonera makanema a ISIS pafoni yake, malinga ndi zambiri zokhudza mlandu wake.
Anapemphanso kuti awonetse mbendera ya ISIS mchipinda chake chachipatala, apolisi atero.
Adakana mlandu 22 yomwe adaimbidwayo.
A David Patton, m'modzi mwa akuimira Saipov, adati "akhumudwitsidwa" ndi chisankho cha oweruza mlandu a boma.
"Tikuganiza kuti lingaliro lofuna kulandira chilango cha imfa m'malo movomera pempho loti akhalebe m'ndende ndikukhala opanda mwayi wotulutsidwa lingawonjezere chisoni kwa aliyense akhudzidwa," adatero Patton.
Maloya a Saipov anali atapempha kale oweruza kuti asapereke chilango cha imfa.
MP akuti NIGEL FARAGE ayenera kuyang'anira zokambirana za Brexit
Nigel Farage adalonjeza kuti 'adzayitanitsa gulu la anthu ngati la nkhondo' lero paziwonetsero pamsonkhano wa Akuluakulu.
Mtsogoleri wakale wa Ukip anati andale ayenera 'kukakamizidwa' kuchokera kwa Otsutsa a EU - monga m'modzi mwa alangizi a Theresa May anati mmeneyo n’oyenera kuyang'anira zokambirana ndi EU.
Peter Bone, yemwe anali wobwerera m'mbuyo, adauza anthu ku Birmingham kuti UK 'ikadakhala itatuluka' pofika pakadali pano ngati a Farage anali Mlembi pa zokambirana za Brexit.
Koma vuto lomwe mayi May akukumana nalo pobwezeretsa magawo omwe agawika kwambiri latsimikiziridwa ndi Osavomerezana ndi Brexit kuti atenge nawo mbali pazionetsero zina zotsutsana ndi Brexit mumzinda.
Mkuluyu akuyesetsa kuti pulani yake yosagwirizana ndi dongosolo laBoma ikhale yabwino potsutsana ndi Ovomerezana ndi Brexit, Ofuna akhale wa E.U komanso bungwe la EU.
Othandizana naye adanenetsa kuti apitilizabe kuyesa kuchita nawo mgwirizano ndi Brussels ngakhale atakumana ndi kutsutsa - ndi kukakamiza Otsutsa a EU ndi a chipani cha Labor kuti asankhe pakati pa zimene akupereka ndi 'chisokonezo'.
A Bone adauza msonkhano wokhala ndi mutu Kuchoka kumatanthauza Kuchoka ku Solihull kuti akufuna 'kutsutsa Otsutsa mgwirizano wa Brexit'.
Ananenanso kuti a Farage akanayenera kutenga nawo gawo ndiponso kupatsidwa udindo wokambirana ndi Brussels.
'Akadakhala kuti ndi mmene akutsogolera nkhaniyi, tikadakhala kuti tidatuluka pofika pano,' anatero.
MP wa Wellingborough adaonjezera kuti: 'Ndithandizira za Brexit koma tikufuna kutsutsa Otsutsa mgwirizano wa Brexit.'
Pofotokoza zotsutsana ndi EU, anati: 'Sitinamenye nkhondo zadziko lonse kuti tikhale akapolo.
Tikufuna kupanga malamulo athu m'dziko lathu lomwelo.'
A Bone adakana mfundo zoti malingaliro a anthu asintha kuyambira pa voti ya 2016: 'Sizoona kuti anthu aku Britain asintha malingaliro awo ndipo akufuna kukhalabe.'
A Brexiteer Andrea Jenkyns nawonso anali pachionetserocho, akuuza atolankhani kuti: 'Ndikungonena kuti: Nduna Yayikulu, mverani anthu.
'Kukhala ku EU sikukufunidwa ndi anthu, Otsutsa sangavomereze izi, sizikufunikanso ndi chipani chathu ndi omenyera omwe amalimbana kwambiri kuti tisankhidwe.
Chonde chokani ku EU ndikuyamba kumvera anthu.'
Kwa mayi May, adawonjezera kuti: 'Akuluakulu monga nduna yayikulu amasunga ntchito zawo akamakwaniritsa malonjezo awo.'
Farage adauza omvera pamsonkhanowu kuti andale ayenera 'kukakamizidwa' ngati ali osakhulupirika pazisankho zaku 2016.
Tsopano ndi nkhani yodalirika pakati pathu - anthu - ndi gulu lathu lazandale,' anatero.
'Akuyesera kukhala osakhulupirika pa nkhani yokhudza Brexit ndipo tili pano lero kuti tiwauze kuti 'sitikulolani kuti muchite izi'.'
Mu uthenga wake ku gulu losangalatsalo adawonjezera kunena kuti: 'Ndikufuna kuti mukakamize andale athu, omwe ali ndi malingaliro osadalirika pankhani ya Brexit.
'Tikuyitanitsa gulu la anthu adzikoli ngati la nkhondo limene linatimenyera nkhondo pankhani yokhudza Brexit ndipo sitidzapumula kufikira titakhala United Kingdom wodziyimira pawokha, waulere komanso wonyada.'
Pakadali pano, akumenyera nkhondo kuti akhale mu bungwe la EU adadutsa ku Birmingham asanakachite msonkhano wamaola awiri pakatikati pa mzindawu.
Otsutsa angapo adakweza zikwangwani zolembedwa kuti Wotsutsa Brexit atakhazikitsa gululi sabata ino.
Msonkhanowu udatsegulidwa mnzake wachipani cha Labour a Lord Adonis adanyoza a chipani cha Conservatives pankhani yokhudza zachitetezo zomwe adakumana nazo ndi pulogalamu yawo ya kompyuta.
'Awa ndi anthu omwe amatiuza kuti atha kukhazikitsa za dongosolo la IT m’dziko komanso ukadaulo wonse ku Canada kuphatikiza, malire opanda zisokonezo, kugulitsa mwa ulere popanda malire ku Ireland,' adaonjeza.
'Ndi nthabwala yathunthu.
Palibe chabwino kuposa Brexit,' anawonjezera.

Purezidenti Donald Trump adanyoza Senator Dianne Feinstein pamsonkhano Loweruka chifukwa choumiriza kuti sanatulutse kalata yochokera kwa a Christine Blasey Ford kuimba mlandu Wosankhidwa ku Khothi Lalikulu Brett Kavanaugh za chiwerewere.

"Chinthu chimodzi chomwe chingachitike ndipo chabwino kwambiri chomwe chitha kuchitika masiku angapo apitawa ku Senate ndikuti, mukawona mkwiyo, mukawona anthu ankhanza komanso okwiya komanso oyipa komanso onama," anatero.
"Tangoonani nkhani yobisika yomwe yatuluka pa mbalambandayi, koma umva akuti "iiii, ine sindinachite zimenezi.
Sindinachite zimenezi."
Mwakumbukira?
Kodi a Dianne Feistein, ndinu munazitulutsa poyera?
Mwakumbukira zomwe anayankha… ndinu munazitulutsa poyera - "iiii, iiii, chiyani?
Iiiii, ayi ndithu.
Sindine ndinatulutsa poyera."
Chabwino, tinene chonchi.
Tinazitulutsa poyera ndife?… Ayi, sindife," adawonjezera motelo a Trump pakulankhula, zomwe zimaonetseratu kuti amakamba za senetiyu.
A Feinstein anatumizilidwa kalata yofotokoza tsatanetsatane wa mulandu wa a Kavanaugh womwe udadza ndi a Ford m’mwezi wa July m’mbuyomo, ndipo nkhaniyi inaululika poyera m’mwezi wa September - koma a Feinstein adakana zoti kuululikaku kudachokera mu ofisi yawo.
"Sindinabise kalikonse pa nkhani imene inadza ndi a Ford, ine sindinayiulutse poyera," a Feinstein anawuza Komiti ya Seneti malingana ndi zomwe nyuzipepala ya The Hill idalemba.
"Adandiuza kuti ikhale nkhani ya chinsinsi ndipo ndidasunga chinsinsi."

Mwina sadachitedi, koma inali njira yoyipitsa yolankhula pogwiritsa zizindikiro za thupi yomwe ndidawonapo."

"Cholinga chawo afuna kubweza mphamvu pogwiritsa ntchito njira ili yonse.

Za Chikho Chachikulu cha Mpira: Dundee Stars 5-3 Belfast Giants
Patrick Dwyer anamwetsa zigoli ziwiri za timu ya Giants motsutsana ndi Dundee
Timu ya Dundee Stars inabweza chipongwe pamene inagonjetsa timu ya Belfast Giants ndi zigoli 5 kwa 3 m’masewera a chibweleza pa bwalo lawo Loweluka lapitali.
Kumayambiliro a masewerowa timu ya Belfast Giants inatsogola ndi zigoli ziwiri kudzera mwa Patrick Dwyer komanso Francis Beauvillier.
Koma timu ya Dundee inabweza zigoli ziwirizi kudzera mwa Mike Sullivan ndi Jordan Cownie kenako Dwyer wa timu ya Belfast Giants anaitsogozanso timu yake kachikena.
Francois Bouchard anagoletsa chigoli chidachita ma timuwa akhale ndi zigoli zofanana kenako Lukas Lundvald Nielsen anagoletsanso zigoli ziwiri zimene zinabweletsa chipambano ku timu ya Dundee Stars.
Kunali kugonjetsedwa kwachitatu mu masewera a Elite League m’nyengoyo kwa amuna a Adam Keefe, omwe adachokera kumbuyo kudzamenya Dundee 2-1 ku Belfast Lachisanu usiku.
Anali masewera achinayi wanyengoyi pakati pa ma timu amenewa, kenako timu ya Giants idapambana masewera atatu am’mbuyo.
Chigoli choyamba cha Dwyer chidabwera mu mphindi ya chinayi pamene panadutsa phindi 3:35 kudzera mwa Kendall McFaull, chigoli china chachiwiri chinachokera kwa Beauvillier kudzera mwa David Rutherford patangopitanso mphindi zinayi kuchoka pa chigoli choyambacho.
Inali nthawi yotsegulira yotanganidwa kwambiri, pamene Sullivan adabwezeretsanso osewera pakhomowa pa 13:10, Matt Marquardt asanaperekere Cownie mwayi womwetsa chigoli chimene chinachititsa kuti ma timuwa akhale ndi zigoli zofanana pa 15:16.
Dwyer adalimbikitsa timu ya Giants pakupuma koyamba pomwe anamenya chigoli chake chachiwiri pa masewera a usikuwa kumapeto kwa nthawi yoyamba.
Timu ya Dundee yomwenso inali pakhomo pawo inadza nzeru zina ndipo Bouchard anamwetsa chigoli chofananira champhamvu pamphindi wa ya 27:37 .
Cownie ndi Charles Corcoran adasewera mwaluso mkupereka mpira kwa Nielsen yemwe adamwetsa chigoli cha Dundee chomwe chinapangitsa kuti timuyi itsogole kwa nthawi yoyamba ku mapeto kwa chigawo chachiwiri ndipo adawonjeza kumwetsanso china zomwe zinafikitsa zigoli zonse pa zisanu m’masewerawa.
Timu ya Giants yomwe tsopano yagonja masewero anayi pa masewero asanu omwe yasewera motsatizana, ikukonzekera zokumana ndi timu ya Milton Keynes pamasewero omwe akudza Lachisanu likubwerali.

Kugwa kwa ndege ku Micronesia: Kampani ya ndege yotchedwa Air Niugini yalengeza kuti munthu m’modzi sakupezekabe ndege itagwera m’madzi
Kampaniyi, yomwe ndi eni wake a ndege yomwe yagwera mu ka gawo ka Nyanja ya mchere ya Pacific, alengezanso kuti munthu modzi sakupezekabe, atalenga pachiyambi kuti onse anakwera ndegeyi anapulumutsidwa pamene ndegeyi imamira.
Kampani ya ndege ya Air Niugini inalengeza kuti pofika nthawi masana tsiku Loweluka, inapeza kuti munthu m’modzi wachizibambo wasowa.
Ndipo inati pakadalipano ikugwira ntchito limodzi ndi atsogoleri akudelako, azaumoyo komanso akatswiri a zofufuza, pa ntchito yosaka mzibambo yemwe wasowayi.
Kampaniyi sidayankhepo kanthu ngati ikudziwapo zambili za mzibambo osowayi, monga zaka zake kapena dziko lomwe amachokera.
Eni ma boti mu deralo adachita machawi populumutsa anthu ndegeyi itangogwera m’madzi pamene imati izitela pa bwalo la ndege la chilumba cha Chuuk.
Akuluakulu ena alengeza kuti anthu okwanira asanu ndi awiri anawatengere ku chipatala.
Kampani ya ndegeyi yati okwera okwana asanu ndi m’modzi adali asanatulutsidwebe m’chipatala Lowerukali, koma onse anali akupeza bwino.
Chenicheni chidayambitsa ngoziyi sichinapezekebe komanso mmene ngoziyi idachitikira.
Kampani ya Ndegeyi komanso asilikali a nkhondo ya pa madzi a dziko la U.S anena kuti ndegeyi inagwera m’madzi itangotsala pang’ono kuti itere pa bwalo la ndege.
Mboni zina zidaganiza kuti ndegeyo idadutsa msewupo.
Okwera nawo ndege, Bill Jaynes wati ndegeyi imaulukira m’musi kwambiri pamene imati itere.
"Ichi ndi chinthu chabwino kwambiri," anatero Jaynes.
Jaynes anati iye ndi ena adakwanitsa kudutsa m'madzi ofika m'chiuno kupita kumalo opulumukira pa ndege yomwe inali ikumira.
Ndipo iye anati othandizira ntchito m’ndegemo amaonetsa kuzingwa ndipo anali kufuula mokweza, anatinso anavulala pang’ono ku mutu.
The U.S. Navy anati oyendetsa boti omwe anali kugwira ntchito pa malo apafupi kukonza bwato anathandiza koposa kupulutsa anthu powatengera ku gombe pogwiritsira ntchito ma boti ndegeyo isaname m'madzi pafupifupi ndimamita 30 (100 feet).

Akatswiri amapereka mndandanda wazomwe zimachitika kufika pa nthawi yomwe mayi ankawotchedwa wamoyo
Wosuma mulandu adaimitsa mlanduwo Loweruka wa bambo yemwe akuimbidwa mlandu wowotcha mkazi wa Mississippi wamoyo mu 2014.
U.S. Department of Justice Analyst Paul Rowlett anachitira umboni kwa maola ambiri ngati mboni yaukatswiri pakusanthula mwanzeru.
Adafotokozera khotilo momwe adagwiritsira ntchito ma foni am'manja kuti aphatikize mayendedwe a womenyera milandu wazaka 29 Quinton Tellis ndi womenyedwa wazaka 19, Jessica Chambers, usiku womwe adamwalira.

Sanford anachitira umboni kuti Loweruka sanali mtawuni tsiku lomwelo.
Oweruza milandu atafunsa ngati Tellis akunena zoona pomwe anati anali mgalimoto ya Sanford usiku womwewo, Sanford anati "akunama, chifukwa galimoto yanga inali ku Nashville nthawi yomweyo."
Kusagwirizana kwina ndikuti Tellis anati adadziwa Chambers pafupifupi milungu iwiri atamwalira.
Umboni kuchokera ku ma foni am'manja akuwonetsa kuti amangodziwana kwa sabata imodzi.
Rowlett anati kanthawi kochepa Chambers atamwalira,Tellis adachotsa zolemba za Chambers, zambiri zakuyimba ndi dzina lake mufoni yake.

Gulu lotchedwa High Breed: Kodi chamba cha nyimbo za hip hapu n’chiyani?
Anthu atatu omwe amaimba chamba cha hip hapu akulingalira zosintha maganizidwe oti chambachi chili ndi zolakwikwa zina poyikamo uthenga wa chilimbikitso mu nyimbo zawo.
Gulu la High Breed, lochokela mu mzinda wa Bristol, lati chamba cha hip hapu chinaleka kumangoimba zokhuza ndale komanso za kukonza mavuto a moyo wathu wa tsiku ndi tsiku.

Munthu wina wakuda?!
Wosamalira ana ku NY akumanga mlandu banja lina chifukwa cha kutumiza uthenga wa "tsankho"
Wosamalira ana ku NY akumanga mlandu banja lina chifukwa cha kutumiza uthenga wa tsankho atalandira uthenga wotayika kuchokera kwa mayiwo akudandaula kuti anali "munthu wina wakuda."
Banjali limakana kuti ndi atsankho, anati mlanduwu uli ngati "njira ya kuba."
Lynsey Plasco-Flaxman, mayi wa ana awiri, adawonetsa kukhumudwa atazindikira kuti wosamalira ana watsopanoyu, Giselle Maurice, anali wakuda atafika tsiku lake loyamba kugwira ntchito chaka cha 2016.
"AYIIIIIIIIIIII AMUNTHU WINA WA KUDA," anatero Mayi Plasco-Flaxmanto m’kalata yopita kwa mwamuna wake.
Komabe, m'malo motumiza kalatayo kwa mwamuna wake, adatumiza kwa Mayi Maurice, kawiri.
Atazindikira kulakwa kwake, "osakhazikika" Plasco-Flaxm anachotsa ntchito Mlongo Maurice, ponena kuti anali woyang'anira ana awo kale, yemwe anali mbadwa yaku Africa-America, adagwira ntchito yoyipa ndipo m'malo mwake amayembekeza kupeza munthu ochokera kuPhilippines, malinga ndi New York Post.
Mlongo Maurice analipidwa ntchito ya tsiku limodzi kenako anatumizidwa kunyumba ku Uber.
Tsopano, Maurice akumanga mlandu banja limeneli pofuna kulipidwa chifukwa chochotsedwa ntchito, ndipo akufuna kulipidwa ndalama zokwana $350 patsiku kwa miyezi isanu ndi umodzi, ntchito ya konsati yanyimbo yomwe anali kugwira kale, mgwirizano uwu usanachitike.
"Ndikufuna kuwasonyeza, mwawona, inu simumachita zinthu m’njira imeneyi," adauza Post Lachisanu ndi kuwonjezera kunena kuti "Ndikudziwa kuti ndi tsankho."
Awiriwa adadzitchinjiriza motsutsana ndi zonena kuti ndi atsankho, ponena kuti kuchotsa ntchito Maurice chinali chinthu chanzeru kuchita, powopa kuti sangamukhulupirire atamukhumudwitsa.
"Mkazi wanga adamutumizira china chake chomwe samafuna kunena.
Iye si watsankho.
Sindife anthu atsankho," mwamuna Joel Plasco adauza a Post.
"Koma kodi mungaike ana anu m'manja mwa munthu amene mwamchitira zoyipa, ngakhale sizinali mwadala?
Mwana wanu watsopano?
Inu anthu."
Pofanizira mlanduwu ndi "njira ya kuba," Plasco anati mkazi wake anali atangotsala ndi miyezi iwiri yokha kuti akhale ndi mwana ndipo anali " m’nthawi yovuta kwambiri."
"Kodi ungatuluke kukamenyana ndi munthu amene ali mumkhalidwewo?
Si chinthu chabwino kwambiri kuchita," wochita bizinesi la mabanki adawonjezera.
Pomwe mlanduwu udakalipobe, khothi lakuwunika kwa anthu mwachangu ladzudzula banjali pasocial media, ndikuwadzudzula chifukwa cha machitidwe awo komanso malingaliro awo.
Ofalitsa buku la Paddington amawopa kuti owerenga sangayerekeze m’maganizo awo zokhudza chimbalangondo chomwe chikuyankhula, kalata yatsopano iulula zimenezi.
Karen Jankel, mwana wamkazi wa Bond, yemwe adabadwa bukuli litavomerezedwa, adanena zokhudza kalatayo kuti: "Ndizovuta kuyika wina m'malo mwa munthu amene amawerenga bukuli koyamba lisanatulutsidwe.
Ndizosangalatsa kudziwa tsopano zomwe tikudziwa zakupambana kwakukulu kwa buku limeneli la Paddington"
Ponena za abambo ake, wojambula wakale wa BBC asanalimbikitsidwe kuti alembe buku la ana ndi chidole chimbalangondo chaching'ono, zingakhale zoyipa kuti atayidwe, ndikuwonjeza kuti chikumbutso cha chaka cha 60 chofalitsa mabukuwa chinali "chowawa komanso chokoma" atamwalira chaka chatha.
Buku la Paddington, lomwe amalifotokoza ngati "lofunika kwambiri m'banja mwathu," ndikuonjeza kuti abambo ake anali onyadira kwambiri kuti pamapeto pake adachita bwino.
"Anali munthu wodekha, ndipo sanali munthu wamwano," anatero.
"Koma chifukwa Paddington anali weniweni kwa iye, zinali pafupifupi ngati muli ndi mwana amene amakwaniritsa china chake: mumanyadira nawo ngakhale simuli omwe mwachita zimenezo.
Ndikuganiza kuti adawona kupambana kwa Paddington motere.
Ngakhale zinali zopanga zake komanso malingaliro ake, nthawi zonse amapereka ulemu kwa Paddington mwiniwake."
Mwana wanga wamkazi anali kumwalira ndipo ndinayenera kutsanzika pafoni
Atafika adathamangira ndi mwana wake wamkazi kuchipatala cha Nice Louis Pasteur 2, komwe madokotala adagwira ntchito pachabe poyesa kupulumutsa moyo wake.
"Nad anali kuyimba foni pafupipafupi kuti anene kuti zinali zoyipadi, ndiponso kuti sanayembekezere kuchira," atero a Ednan-Laperouse.

Ndipo ndidatero.
Ndinati, "Tashi, ndimakukonda kwambiri, wokondedwa wanga.
Ndidzakhala nanu posachedwa.
Ndidzakhala nanu.
Mankhwala omwe madotolo adamupatsa kuti azipopa mtima wake anali kutuluka ndi kutha pang'onopang'ono mthupi lake.
Anali atamwalira kale kanthawi kochepa ndipo izi zinali kutseka chabe.
Ndinayenera kukhala pamenepo ndikudikirira, podziwa kuti zonsezi zimachitika.
Sindingathe kulira kapena kukuwa chifukwa ndinali mumkhalidwe wozunguliridwa ndi anthu a m’banja komanso anthu ena.
Ndinafunika kuti ndizisunge ndekha."
Pambuyo pake Mayi Ednan-Laperouse, pakadali pano akumva chisoni ndi imfa ya mwana wawo wamkazi, anakwera ndege limodzi ndi anthu ena - osazindikira mavuto omwe anali nawo.
"Palibe amene amadziwa zimenezo," anatero.
"Mutu wanga unali pansi, ndipo misozi inali kugwa nthawi yonseyo.
Ndizovuta kuzifotokoza, koma panali paulendo womwe ndimamvera chisoni Nad.
Kuti ankafuna chikondi changa komanso kuti nd’mmvetsetse.
Ndinadziwa m'mene amandikondera.”
Amayi achisoni amatumiza makadi kuti apewe kudzipha pa mlatho
Amayi awiri omwe abale awo adamwalira chifukwa chodzipha akuyesetsa kuti ena asadziphe.
Sharon Davis ndi Kelly Humphreys akhala akutumiza makadi pa mlatho wa Welsh wokhala ndi mauthenga olimbikitsa komanso manambala a foni omwe anthu amatha kuyimba akafuna thandizo.
Tyler, mwana wamwamuna wa Mlongo Davis anali ndi zaka 13 pomwe adayamba kuvutika ndi nkhawa ndipo adadzipha ali ndi zaka 18.
"Sindikufuna kholo lililonse kumva momwe ndimamvera tsiku ndi tsiku," anatero.
Mayi Davis, wazaka 45, yemwe amakhala ku Lydney, anati mwana wawo wamwamuna anali ndi mwayi wokhala wophika wabwino yemwe amamwetulira kwambiri.
"Aliyense ankamudziwa chifukwa cha kumwetulira kwake.
Nthawi zonse amati kumwetulira kwake kumawunikira malo aliwonse."
Komabe, adasiya ntchito asanamwalire, popeza anali "pamavuto kwambiri."
Mu 2014, mchimwene wake wa Tyler, yemwe anali 11 panthawiyo, ndiye amene adamupeza m'bale wake atadzipha.
Mayi Davis anati: "Ndimakhala ndi nkhawa kuti padzakhala zotsatira zabwino."
Mlongo Davis adapanga makhadiwo, "kuti anthu adziwe kuti pali anthu kunja komwe omwe mungapiteko ndipo mumatha kukambirana nawo, ngakhale ndi bwenzi.
Osangokhala chete - muyenera kuyankhula."
Mayi Humphreys, yemwe anali mnzake wa Amayi Davies kwazaka zambiri, mwamuna wake Mark anamwalira, mnzake wazaka 15, pasanapite nthawi amayi ake atamwaliranso.
"Sananene kuti akumva kukhumudwa kapena chisoni kapena chilichonse," anatero.
"Masiku angapo Khrisimasi isanachitike tidawona momwe amasinthira.
Sanali bwino kwenikweni patsiku la Khrisimasi - ana atatsegula mphatso zawo sanayang'ane nawo kapena kunena chilichonse."
Anatinso kuti imfa yake inali yowawopsa kwambiri, koma akuyenera kupirira mu izi: "Zinasiya am’banja akuvutika kwambiri.
Zimatilekanitsa.
Koma tonse tiyenera kupitiliza ndikupirira."

Tsogolo la Brett Kavanaugh silikudziwika pamene FBI iyamba kufufuza
"Ndinaganiza kuti, ngati titapeza chilichonse chonga chomwe amafunsira - monga kafukufuku wa nthawi ifupi, wochepa pamlingo - tikhoza mwina kubweretsa umodzi pang'ono," a Flake adatero Loweruka, anaonjezera kuti anaopa komitiyi inali "kugwa" mkati mwa nkhondo yolimba yazandale.
Kodi n’chifukwa chiyani a Kavanaugh ndi omutsatira aku Republican sankafuna kuti FBI ifufuze?
Kukana kwawo kumachitika chifukwa cha zinthu zomwe zinali pafupi kuchitika.
Zisankho zapakatikati zatsala ndi milungu isanu kuti zichitidwe, pa Novembara 6 -ngati, monga zikuyembekezeredwa, a chipani cha Republican alephera, ndiye adzafooka kwambiri poyesera kuti abweretse munthu yemwe akufuna kuti am’sankhe kukhothi lalikulu m’dzikolo.
A George W. Bush akhala akutenga foni kuti ayimbire a ku Seneti, kuwalimbikitsa kuti athandizire a Kavanaugh, yemwe ankagwira ntchito ku White House nthawi ya a Bush ndipo kudzera mwa iye a Bush adakumana ndi mkazi wawo Ashley, yemwe anali mlembi wawo.
Kodi chidzachitike n’chiyani FBI itatulutsa lipoti lake?
Padzakhala voti ku Senate, komwe kuli ndi mmembala 51 a chipani cha Republican ndi ma membala 49 a chipani cha Democrat.
Sizikudziwika ngati a Kavanaugh atha kupeza mavoti osachepera 50 kunyumba ya Senate, zomwe zingalole Mike Pence, wachiwiri kwa purezidenti, kuti athetse nkhaniyi ndikumutsimikizira ku Khothi Lalikulu.
Chiwerengero cha opanduka "chatsika" motsogozedwa ndi Kim
Chiwerengero cha omwe akuchokera ku North Korea n’kupanduka kuti akhale nzika za ku South Korea chatsika kuyambira Kim Jong-un atayamba kulamulira zaka zisanu ndi ziwiri zapitazo, wopanga malamulo ku South Korea atero.
A Park Byeong-seug, akunena zokhudza zambiri kuchokera ku ofesi ya nduna ya zamgwirizano ku South, adati panali 1,127 chaka chatha - poyerekeza ndi 2,706 mu 2011.
Park adati kuyang’aniridwa bwino kwa malire a pakati pa dziko la North Korea ndi dziko la China komanso mitengo yokwera yomwe ozembetsa amalipiritsa n’zifukwa zakutsika kumeneku.
Pyongyang sananene chilichonse pa nkhaniyi.
Ambiri opanduka ochokera ku North Korea pamapeto pake amapatsidwa chilolezo chokhala nzika zaku South Korea.
Seoul akuti anthu aku North Korea opitilira 30,000 adadutsa malire mosaloledwa kuyambira kumapeto kwa nkhondo yaku Korea m’chaka cha 1953.
Ambiri amathawa kudzera ku China, komwe kuli ndi malire ataliatali ndi North Korea ndipo n’kosavuta kuwoloka kuposa Malo Otetezedwa Kwambiri a Demilitarized Zone (DMZ) pakati pa mayiko a Koreya awiriwa.
China imawona opandukawa ngati osamukira mosaloledwa m'malo mothawa kwawo ndipo nthawi zambiri amawabwezera mokakamiza.
Ubale pakati pa North Korea ndi South Korea - womwe adakali pankhondo - wasintha kwambiri miyezi yapitayi.
Kumayambiriro kwa mwezi uno, atsogoleri awiriwa adakumana ku Pyongyang kuti akambirane za zida za nyukiliya zokambirana zomwe zidalephera m'mbuyomu.
Izi zidachitika pambuyo pa msonkhano wapadera wa Juni pakati pa Purezidenti wa US a Donald Trump ndi Kim Jong-un ku Singapore, pomwe awiriwa adavomerana motere kuti agwire ntchito yowononga zida zonse za nyukiliya mu mayiko awo a ku Korea.
Koma Loweruka, Nduna Yowona Zakunja yaku North Korea a Ri Yong-ho adati zilango zochokera kudziko la US ndi zimene zikusokoneza mayendedwe abwino a zinthu kuyambira pamenepo.
"Popanda kukhulupirira dziko la America sitidzakhala okhutira ndi chitetezo cha dziko lathu ndipo muzinthu izi sizingatheke kuti ife tiyambirire kusiya kugwiritsa ntchito zida za nyukiliya tokha," a Ri atero polankhula ku UN General Assembly ku New York.
Nancy Pelosi amatcha Brett Kavanaugh "wamisala," akuti ndiwosayenerera kutumikira ku Khothi Lalikulu
Mtsogoleri wokhala ndi mamembala ochepa a paliament Nancy Pelosi akuti Wosankhidwa ku Khothi Lalikulu Brett Kavanaugh "wamisala" ndipo adati alibe nzeru zogwirira ntchito ku Khothi Lalikulu.
Pelosi wanena izi poyankhulana kunachitika Loweruka ku Texas Tribune Festival ku Austin, Texas.
"Sindingathe kuchita china koma ndikuganiza kuti ngati mkazi adachitapo izi, akanati 'wamisala,' "adatero Pelosi popereka maganizo ake okhudza zimene Kavanaugh akanena ngati umboni pamaso pa Komiti Yoweruza ya Senate Lachinayi.
Kavanaugh adakana milandu yoti adagwiririra Dr. Christine Blasey Ford pamene onse anali achichepere.
M'mawu ake oyamba, Kavanaugh anali wokhumudwa kwambiri, nthawi zina ankangofuula ndikutsamwa pokambirana za banja lake komanso nthawi yake ya kusekondale.
Anadzudzulanso a chipani cha Democrats pa komitiyi, ponena kuti zomwe amunenezazi ndi "zoyipa komanso zoyeserera kuyipisa dzina la munthu" zokonzedwa ndi anthu omasuka omwe adakwiya kuti Hillary Clinton sanapambane chisankho cha 2016.
Pelosi adati amakhulupirira kuti umboni wa Kavanaugh udatsimikizira kuti sayenera kugwira ntchito ku Khothi Lalikulu, chifukwa zidawonetsa kuti akukondera chipani cha Democrats.
"Ndikuganiza kuti amadzichotsera ntchito ndi zimene akanena komanso momwe amalankhulira Clintons ndi ma Democrat," anatero.
Pelosi adakayikira atafunsidwa ngati angayesere kuchotsa ntchito Kavanaugh mnjira ya voti ngati atatsimikiziridwa ntchitoyo, komanso ngati ma Democrat apeza mamembala ambiri m’nyumba ya Oyimira.
"Zimene ndinganene n’zakuti - ngati sanena zowona ku Congress kapena ku FBI, ndiye kuti sali woyenera kukhala ku Khothi Lalikulu, koma kuti akhale kubwalo lomwe ali pano, "anatero Pelosi.
Kavanaugh pakadali pano ndi woweruza ku DC Circuit Court of Appeals.
Pelosi adaonjezeranso kuti ngati membala wa chipani cha Democrat anali ndi nkhawa ndi zigamulo zomwe Kavanaugh angatsutse zokhudza dongosolo la Affordable Care Act kapena Roe v. Wade, popeza amamuwona ngati loya wachipani cha Democrat.
Pazomvera zake zotsimikizira, a Kavanaugh adapewa mafunso okhudza ngati angasinthe zigamulo zina ku Khothi Lalikulu.
"Ino si nthawi yoti munthu wamisala, wokondera apite kukhothi ndipo akayembekezere kuti tinene kuti, 'sizabwino zoterezi,' "anatero Pelosi.
Ndipo Akazi Ayenera Kuigwiritsa Ntchito Bwino Njirayi.

Chimodzi mwazinthu zomwe ndimakumbukira kwambiri pantchito yanga yoyamba, ndinali muofesi ili ndi amuna ambiri, komwe nthawi ina ndinapezeka ndikulira ndi ukali wosaneneka, kunali kugwidwa kwanga ndi mayi wachikulire - manejala wofatsa yemwe nthawi zonse ndinkachita naye mantha pang'ono - yemwe adandikokera kukwera masitepe.
"Musalole anthuwa kuti akuwoneni mukulira," anandiuza kutero.
"Sakudziwa kuti wakwiya.
Akuganiza kuti ndinu achisoni ndipo akusangalala kuti abwera kwa inu."
A Patricia Schroeder, omwe kale anali Democratic Congress ku Colorado, adagwirapo ntchito ndi a Gary Hart pa kampeni yawo ya Purezidenti.
Mu 1987, a Hart atagwidwa akuchita za chigololo atakwera boti lotchedwa Monkey Business zimene zinachititsa kuti achoke pa mpikisano, Schroede, wokhumudwitsidwa kwambiri, adaganiza kuti palibe chifukwa chomwe sayenera kufufuza lingaliro loti atenge nawo gawo pa mpikisano pomenyera kukhala ngati purezidenti.
"Sanasankhe bwino, "adandiuza ndikuseka zaka 30 pambuyo pake.
"Panali kale ena asanu ndi awiri ofuna kulowa nawo mpikisano, ndipo chotsiriza chomwe amafunikira anali munthu m'modzi.
Wina wake adazitcha "Snow White ndi Seven Dwarfs.""
Chifukwa inali kampeni yochitidwa mwadzidzidzi, anali kumbuyo pakupanga ndalama, ndipo adatsimikiza kuti sangatenge nawo mpikisanowu pokhapokha atapeza ndalama zokwanira $2 miliyoni.
Uku kudali kulephera.
Adapeza kuti ena mwa omuthandiza omwe adapereka $1,000 kwa amuna ayenera kumupatsa $250 yokha.
"Kodi akuganiza kuti ndimalandira kuchotsera?" adadabwa nazo.
Atalengeza kuti sakukhazikitsa kampeni yeniyeni, zinamukhudza kwambiri - kuthokoza anthu omwe amuthandiza, kukhumudwitsidwa ndimakonzedwe a zinthu omwe adapangitsa kuti zikhale zovuta kupeza ndalama ndi makonzedwe olimbana ndi anthu amafuna kuvota osati owayimira, ndi kukwiya chifukwa cha kusalidwa - zichititsa kuti atsale pang'ono kulira.
"Mukadaganiza kuti ndinali pamavuto akulu," Mayi Schroeder akukumbukira momwe atolankhani amamuchitira.
"Mukadaganizira kuti Kleenex anali wothandizira kampani yanga.
Ndimakumbukira ndikuganiza kuti, adzaika chiyani pamwala wanga wamanda?
"Analira"?""
Kuunika za momwe dziko la China lingapindulire Kamba ka kulimbana pakati pa dzikoli ndi dziko la Ameleka.
Chiyambi cha kulimbanaku chinali chopatsa mantha komanso kuchititsa jenkha. Pakali pano kulimbanaku kukadali mkati koma akadaulo omwe akuitsata bwino nkhaniyi apeza kuti mpungwepungwewu utha kuchitila ubwino dziko la China kumapeto kwa zonse.
Chiyambi cha izi chidadza pamene mtsogoleri wa dziko la Ameleka, a Donald Trump anakhazikitsa misonkho pa katundu mkulumkulu ochoka m’dziko la China monga zipangizo zopangila magetsi a dzuwa, zitsulo zosiyanasiyana kuphatikizapo za aluminiyamu.
Kulimbanaku kunaoneka kuti kwafika pa mpondachimera mu sabata limeneli pamene dziko la Ameleka linalamula kuti katundu wankhaninkhani wa ndalama zokwana 200 biliyoni dolazi ya Amereka, kapena mwa njira ina zokwana 150 biliyoni paundi ya Britain.
Nalo dziko la China lakhala likubwezera chipongwechi ku dziko la Amereka pokhazikitsa misonkho yawo yofuna kukhaulitsa dziko la Amereka, posachedwapa inakhazikitsa misonkho ya pakati pa maperesenti asanu ndi khumi ndiponso misonkhoyi inali kukhudza katundu wa ndalama zokwana ma dola 60 bilioni wa dziko la Amereka.
Dziko la China lanenetsa kuti libwezela chipongwechi mogwirizana ndi mmene dziko la Amereka lingachitile ndipo likhala ndi tcheru pa nkhaniyi.
Kuti dziko la Amereka lisiye nchitidwewu, zikufunika kuti katundu ochokera ku dziko la China asiye kukhala otsika mtengo kwambili ndi wachikoka ku dziko la Amereka koma kuti dziko la China ligonjele poyera ndi zovuta chifukwa zitha kubweletsa chitonzo pa mtsogoleri wa dzikolo, a Xi Jinping.
Komabe, akatswiri ena anena kuti mpungwepungwewu utha kuthandizira China kwanthawi yayitali pochepetsa kudalirana kwa mayiko awiriwa, zimenezi zikhoza kuchitika ngati dziko la China lachita chisankho chabwino.
"Abgail Grace, yemwe akugwira ndi bungwe la Center for New America Security, yemwenso ndi katswiri wa za kafukufuku okhuza maiko a Asia, anati "ziganizo zopangidwa mwachangu kamba ka zifukwa za ndale zili ndi kuthekela kosokoneza ntchito za chuma m’maiko a Amereka komanso China mopitilira muyezo kuposera mmene ena amaganizila".
Syria "yakonzeka" kuti othawa abwerere, atero Unduna wa Zakunja
Syria yati ili okonzeka kubwerera kwa othawa kwawo ndipo ikupempha thandizo kuti amangenso dziko lomwe lakhala likuwonongedwa ndi nkhondo ya zaka zoposa zisanu ndi ziwiri.
Polankhula ku United Nations General Assembly, Nduna Yowona Zakunja Walid al-Moualem anati zinthu zikuyamba kuyenda bwino mdziko.
"Pakadali pano zinthu zakhazikika komanso zotetezeka chifukwa cha zomwe zachitika polimbana ndi uchigawenga," anatero
Boma likupitiliza kukonzanso malo omwe awonongedwa ndi zigawenga kuti abwezeretse chikhalidwe chabwino.
Zinthu zonse zakhazikika pakadalipano kwa othawa kuti abwere kudziko lomwe amayenera kuchoka chifukwa cha uchigawenga komanso njira zachuma zomwe zidakhudza miyoyo yawo tsiku ndi tsiku komanso khalidwe lawo.
UN ikuyerekeza kuti anthu aku Syria oposa 5.5 miliyoni adathawa mdzikolo kuyambira pomwe nkhondo idayamba mchaka cha 2011.
Anthu enanso sikisi miliyoni omwe akukhalabe mdzikolo akufuna thandizo.
Al-Moualem anati boma la Syria lilandila thandizo pomanganso dziko lowonongedwali.
Koma adanenetsa kuti silingalandire thandizo lili ndi zofunikira zina kapena thandizo kuchokera kumayiko omwe adathandizira zigawengazo.
Timu ya Europe ndiyo yatenga chikho cha masewero a gofo cha Ryder Cup mu Paris
Timu ya Europe yatenga chikho cha Ryder Cup cha m’chaka cha 2018 itagonjetsa timu ya USA ndi ma pointi 16 ndi theka kwa 10 ndi theka pa galaundi la Le Gold National, kunja kwa mzinda wa Paris, mdziko la France.
Dziko la Amereka lakhala likugonja pa masewero a Ryder Cup kwa zaka zisanu ndi chimodzi zotsatizana zimene akhala akusewerera ku maiko a ku Ulaya komanso timuyi sinatengepo chikhochi kuyambila chaka cha 1993.
Timu ya maiko a ku ulayayi yomwe otsogolera osewera anzake ndi Thomas Bjorn, inatenga chikhochi mobweleza itakwanitsa kupeza zigoli 14.5 kuti igonjetse timu ya dziko la United States.
Katswiri wa timu ya US, Phil Mickelson, yemwe anakanika kuonetsa chamuna pa mpikisanowu adaponyera mpira mukadzenje kosayenera zimene zinapangitsa kuti m’dani wake Francesco Molinari, apeze danga lowagonjetsera.
Osewera ochokera ku dziko la Italy adasewera mopatsa kaso m’magawo onse a masewerawa izi n’kupangitsa iye kukhala 1 mwa osewera 4 omwe anagoletsa 5-0-0 chiyambile mpikisano wamasewerawu mu chaka cha 1979.
Osewera wa Amereka, Jordan Spieth sadaothele pamene anagonja ndi ma pointi 5&4 kwa osewera wa timu ya ku Ulaya Thorbjorn Olesen ochokera m’dziko la Denmark, yemwe sanafike pa ukatswiri weniweni.
Wosewera wodziwika kwambiri padziko lonse lapansi, Dustin Johnson, adagwa 2 ndi 1 kwa Ian Poulter waku England yemwe mwina amasewera masewera ake omaliza mu chikho cha Ryder Cup chi.
Wampikisano wa Ryder Cups, Spaniard Sergio Garcia wakhala wosewera wopambana kwambiri ku Europe ndi mapointi 25.5 panthawi yomwe anali wosewera.
"“Ine kulira sikwenikweni koma na lero lokha sindingachitile mwina.
Ichi chinali chaka chovuta kwambiri.
Ndili othokoza mphunzitsi wathu Thomas pondisakha ndi kundikhulupilira .
Ndine wokondwa kwambiri, ndikusangalala kuti ndalandiranso chikhochi.
Cholinga chinali kuti timu yathu ipambane., ndipo ndine okondwa kuti ndatenga nawo mbali pa kupambana kumeneku," adatelo Garcia yemwe amaoneka okodwa kwambiri potsatira kupambana kwa timu yake ya ku Ulaya.
Anathokoza nzika mnzake a John Ram omwe adagonjetsa US Tiger Woods 2&1 pamasewera a m'modzi ndi m'modzi Lamlungu.
"Ndine onyadira koposa pogonjetsa katswiri Tiger Woods, m’mene ndimakula ndikuonera iyeyu akusewera," anatero Rahm, wa zaka 23.
Woods adagonja pa masewero onse anayi mu France ndipo pano wakwanitsa kupeza chipambano mu mpikisano wa Ryder Cup chomwe chafika pa 13-21-3.
Izi ndi zoimitsa mutu polingalira kuti mmeneyu ndi m'modzi mwa akatswiri a mdziko lapansi, amene wapambana mipikisano yokwana 14 ndipo amangoposedwa ndi Jack Nicklaus yekha.
Timu USA idavutika kumapeto kwa sabata yonse kuti ipeze zotsatira zabwino kupatulapo a Patrick Reed, Justin Thomas ndi Tony Finau, omwe adasewera gofu wapamwamba pamasewera onse.
Woyang'anira wamkulu waku US a Jim Furyk adalankhula atachita masewera okhumudwitsa pagulu lake, "Ndine wonyadira za anyamatawa, agwira ntchito molimbika.
Panali nthawi m'mawa uno pomwe tavutitsa timu yaku Europe.
Nkhondo tinamenya ndithu.
Ulemu onse upite kwa Thomas.
Ndiwotsogolera bwino.
Osewera ake onse 12 asewera bwino kwambiri.
Tidzipanganso zina, nditha kugwira ntchito ndi PGA of America ndi Komiti yathu ya Ryder Cup ndipo tidzapita patsogolo.
Anzanga onsewa 12 ndimawakonda ndipo ndine onyadira pokhala mtsogoleri wawo.
Titha kunena kuti mutsale bwino.
Tivomereze kuti anzathu anasewera bwino kupambana ife."
Zambiri Zokhudza Mafunde Ofiira: Kuchuluka kumachepa ku Pinellas, Manatee ndi Sarasota
Lipoti laposachedwa kuchokera ku Khomishoni ya Nsomba ndi Nyama Zakutchire ku Florida likuwonetsa kuchepa kwakukulu kwa kuchuluka kwa Red Tide m'malo ena a Tampa Bay.
Malinga ndi FWC, magawo a mafunde ofiira akupezeka m'malo a Pinellas, Manatee, Sarasota, Charlotte ndi Collier - zomwe zikuwonetsa kuchepa kwa kuchuluka.
Kuphulika kwa Mafunde Ofiira kumatalika pafupifupi ma mayilo 130 ma magombe kuchokera kumpoto kwa Pinellas kupita kum'mwera kwa Lee.
Zigawo zimapezekanso ma mayilo 10 kumtunda kwa Hillsborough County, koma m'malo ochepera poyelekeza ndi sabata yatha.
Mafunde Ofiira adawonekanso ku Pasco County.
Kuchuluka kwapakati pagombe la Pinellas County kunanenedwa sabata yatha, kuchuluka kung’ono komanso kokwela kumtunda kwa Hillsborough County, kuchuluka kwa pafupi komanso kukulu ku Manatee County, kuchuluka kwa pafupi komanso kukulu kumtunda kwa Sarasota County, kuchuluka kung’ono komanso kwa pafupi ku Charlotte County, kuchuluka kwa pafupi komanso kukulu kumtunda kwa Lee County, ndi kuchuluka kung’ono ku Collier County.
Vuto la kupuma likupitilizabe kunenedwa m'matauni a Pinellas, Manatee, Sarasota, Lee, ndi Collier.
Vuto la kupuma silunenedwe ku Northwest Florida sabata yathayi.
